import evgsus as es

#tech that i know
es.tech_stack( linux(ubuntu, centos), python3(), git(github, gitlab))

class Current_study():
 def __init__(self, color, zabbix, Docker, Kubernets:
        self.color = yellow #my favorite color
        self.zabbix = zabbix
        self.Docker = docker
        self.Kubernets  = kubernets
    
    def zabbix (self):
        #monitoring
        return "Studying"
    
    def docker(self):
        #container stuff
        return "I'm trying!"
        
    def kubernets(self):
        #orchestration
        return "It's like a musik"
